	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Quickstart guide</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Dwarf Fortress Wiki</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div id="page-quality-rating" style="text-align: right;margin: 0.8em 0;font-size:75%">
 <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:Quality#Tattered" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:Quality"><span id="stub-quality" style="text-decoration:none; color:#333333">xTATTEREDx</span></a> <span style="font-weight:bold;" class="dot">&#160;·</span> <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:Quality#Fine" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:Quality"><span id="fine-quality" style="text-decoration:none; color:#CA7A02;">+FINE+</span></a> <span style="font-weight:bold;" class="dot">&#160;·</span> <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:Quality#Superior" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:Quality"><span id="superior-quality" style="text-decoration:none; color:#8800cc;">*SUPERIOR*</span></a> <span style="font-weight:bold;" class="dot">&#160;·</span> <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:Quality#Exceptional" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:Quality"><span id="exceptional-quality" style="text-decoration:none; color:#0088CC;">≡EXCEPTIONAL≡</span></a> <span style="font-weight:bold;" class="dot">&#160;·</span> <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:Quality#Masterwork" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:Quality"><span id="masterwork-quality" style="padding:0.2em; border:1px solid #bd8; border-radius: 2px; -webkit-border-radius: 2px; -moz-border-radius: 2px; -o-border-radius: 2px; -ms-border-radius: 2px; background:#E2FDCE; color:#72A329;">☼MASTERWORK☼</span></a></div>
<table class="version-table" style="text-align: center; margin: 3px auto 5px; padding: 0.25em; border-radius: 3px; -webkit-border-radius: 3px; -moz-border-radius: 3px; -o-border-radius: 3px; -ms-border-radius: 3px;; border: 2px solid #bbdd88; background: #f5ffee; min-width:27em"><tbody><tr><td style="padding: 0.3em 0.3em; width: 100%;"><div style="margin-bottom:6px;" class="version-links-r1"><span style="font-size:100%"><span class="version-link"><span style="text-decoration: none; color: #72A329; background-color: #E2FDCE; border-radius: 2px; -webkit-border-radius: 2px; -moz-border-radius: 2px; -o-border-radius: 2px; -ms-border-radius: 2px; border: 1px solid #bbdd88; padding: 0.2em;"><b>v50.14</b></span></span><span style="font-weight:bold;" class="dot">&#160;·</span> <span class="version-link"><a href="/index.php/DF2014:Quickstart_guide" title="DF2014:Quickstart guide"><span style="text-decoration: none; color: #72A329;">v0.47.05</span></a></span></span></div><span>This article is about the current version of DF.<br />Note that some content may still need to be updated.</span><br />
<div style="float: right; font-size:75%; padding-right:2px; margin-top:-2px; margin-bottom:-7px;"><span class="version-link"><a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:V" class="mw-redirect" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:V"><span style="text-decoration: none; color: #72A329;">More Info</span></a></span><span style="font-weight:bold;" class="dot">&#160;·</span> <span class="version-link"><a href="/index.php/Template:Av" class="mw-redirect" title="Template:Av"><span style="text-decoration: none; color: #72A329;">V</span></a></span></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<dl><dd><i>For installation instructions, see <a href="/index.php/Installation" title="Installation">Installation</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>This is a quickstart guide for <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_fortress_mode" title="Dwarf fortress mode">dwarf fortress mode</a> for those who have never played before and quickly want to jump in head-first.</i> <i>If you are looking to learn adventure mode instead, see the <a href="/index.php/Adventure_mode_quick_start" title="Adventure mode quick start">Adventure mode quick start</a> guide.</i></dd>
<dd><i>Also see <a href="/index.php/Tutorials" title="Tutorials">Tutorials</a> for more detailed tutorials that people have submitted.</i></dd></dl>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: #0a0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Before you get started...</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>Always remember that <b>losing is <a href="/index.php/Fun" class="mw-redirect" title="Fun">fun</a>!</b> Be prepared to lose a few fortresses before you get all the way through this guide &#8211; it can be easy to accidentally kill the entire fortress while learning. But remember: losing means that next time, <i><a href="#Situational_Awareness">you'll remember how you lost</a>.</i> In a big way, <i>Dwarf Fortress</i> uses the principle of learning from one's mistakes.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p><br />
So, you want to play <b>Dwarf Fortress</b>, but you have no idea what to do. That's understandable; in <i>Dwarf Fortress</i> you can really do anything you like - it's a huge, complex, and totally open-ended game. But in order to do anything, first you need a sustainable fortress. It turns out that doing this is not as hard as you might think.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:448px;"><a href="/index.php/File:FlowchartDF.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/e/e6/FlowchartDF.png/446px-FlowchartDF.png" decoding="async" width="446" height="571" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/e/e6/FlowchartDF.png/669px-FlowchartDF.png 1.5x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:FlowchartDF.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/index.php/From_Caravan_to_Happy_Dwarves" title="From Caravan to Happy Dwarves">From Caravan to Happy Dwarves</a> - This is a flowchart showing approximately what sequence of actions players usually take when starting up a new fort. Feel free to ignore it if you want. It's not necessary to refer to this to understand the rest of the guide, but by the time you finish the guide it will probably all make sense.</div></div></div>

<h1><span class="mw-headline" id="Common_UI_Concepts">Common UI Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Common UI Concepts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h1>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: #0a0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Keeping Up</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>While the guide contains many links, you may still need to look something up. Refer to the <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_fortress_mode" title="Dwarf fortress mode">Fortress Mode Reference Guide</a> or use the wiki <a href="/index.php/Special:Search" title="Special:Search">search</a> function. Also, don't hesitate to <a href="/index.php/Troubleshooting" title="Troubleshooting">ask for help</a> if you can't find answers on the wiki.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p><br />
This is just the Quickstart Guide, so we skip lots of details on the UI. If you're looking for more UI help as you get deeper into your first fortress, you may also want to read this section in the <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_fortress_mode#Gameplay_user_interface" title="Dwarf fortress mode">Fortress Mode Guide</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="About_key_symbols">About key symbols</span></h2>
<p>This wiki uses symbols that look like <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span> or <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_t.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui t.png" src="/images/5/56/Ui_t.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="36" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span></span></span></span> to indicate what keys or <a href="/index.php/Interface" title="Interface">interface</a> buttons are used for an operation. Note that keys are <b>case sensitive</b> and to save space, <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Shift</span>+<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span> is shown as <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-t">T</span></span>. So <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span> means "press the 't' key without the shift key" and <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-t">T</span></span> means "hold down shift and press the 't' key". Lowercase and uppercase keys will often perform different functions, so it is important to use the correct key. Sequences of keys will be in separate boxes, so <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">a</span><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-c">C</span></span> means "press 'a', then press 'b', then hold shift and press 'c'"; while <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bT.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bT.png" src="/images/9/92/Ui_bT.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-t">T</span></span></span></span></span> means "press 'b', then hold shift and press 'T'. A plus sign '+' between the boxes means to press them all together, so <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Shift</span>+<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Enter</span></span> means to hold shift and press 'Enter'. Other separators, such as ',' or '-', might be used but mean the same as no separator: to press the keys in sequence.
</p><p>Keybindings can be seen and changed on the <a href="/index.php/Settings#Keybindings" title="Settings">Keybindings</a> tab in the <a href="/index.php/Settings" title="Settings">Settings</a> menu.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Menu_navigation_and_selection">Menu navigation and selection</span></h2>

</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> or <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">right mouse</span></span> will almost always return to the previous screen until you get to the top level of the UI, at which point <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> will display the options menu.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Options_menu">Options menu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Options menu">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint relarticle mainarticle"><i>Main article: <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_fortress_mode#Options_screen" title="Dwarf fortress mode">Options screen</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Basic game-related tasks (saving, quitting, settings, etc.) are available on the options menu, which can be reached with <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_Esc.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui Esc.png" src="/images/2/2f/Ui_Esc.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="24" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span></span></span></span> from the main screen. <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> again or <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">right click</span></span> will close the menu. This menu also shows the current or previous music track.
</p><p>For more information see <a href="/index.php/Saved_game_folder#Saving" title="Saved game folder">Saving</a>, <a href="/index.php/Reclaim_fortress_mode" title="Reclaim fortress mode">Reclaim fortress mode</a>, and <a href="/index.php/Settings" title="Settings">Settings</a>.
</p>
<h1><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Generation">World Generation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: World Generation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h1>
<p>First, <a href="/index.php/World_generation" title="World generation">create a new world</a>. <i>Dwarf Fortress</i> worlds are always procedurally randomly generated - there is no "default" or "standard" world. Luckily, the basic version of this process is simple, and with these suggested settings won't take too long. Wait until the game shows that the world has been generated, since stopping history too soon can limit material availability for embark and trade.
</p>
<div style="float: none; clear:both; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: auto; width: 80%;">
<div style="background: #00a; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Starting World</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>For your first game, <a href="/index.php/World_generation" title="World generation">generate a new world</a> using the <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Create new world</span> option in the main menu with the following options:
</p>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">World map size</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Medium</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">History length</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">100 years</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Number of Civilizations</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Medium</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Number of Sites</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Medium</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Number of Beasts</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Low</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Natural Savagery</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Very Low</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Mineral Occurrence</span> at <span style="color: #12FECF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Everywhere</span></li></ul>
</div>
</div>
<p>When it's finished choose <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Play now</span>, the game will save the world and then ask for a game type, choose <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Fortress</span>. The game will then quickly simulate two weeks of world activity and then offer a tutorial.
</p>
<h1><span class="mw-headline" id="Tutorial">Tutorial</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Tutorial">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h1>
<p>The in game tutorial is quite good and it is strongly suggested that new players play through it at least once. It will automatically choose a site for the fortress as well as dwarves and supplies. It will then show you how to use the <a href="/index.php/Interface" title="Interface">interface</a> to strike the earth and get started on your fortress. If a tutorial window is covering a part of the interface you are trying to use, you can roll up the window with the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">^</span></span> button. You can replay any part of the tutorial at any time by pressing the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">?</span></span> button next the minimap; this also provides a list of non-interactive guides on many parts of the game.
</p>
<h1><span class="mw-headline" id="Embark">Embark</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Embark">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h1>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint relarticle mainarticle"><i>Main article: <a href="/index.php/Embark" title="Embark">Embark</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Embarking is the process of choosing a site, outfitting your initial dwarves, and sending them on their way. If you choose to <span style="color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #A2DC34">Start tutorial</span> the game will do it all for you, flashing the location of the site it chose, then skipping straight to your arrival there. It is the quickest way to start.
</p><p>If you choose <span style="color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #FF113A">Skip tutorial</span>, you'll get some good advice not to ignore any warnings about the site. You can then look around by pointing at locations to see details, zoom in with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">left click</span></span>, and zoom out with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">right click</span></span> (if any menu is open right click closes it instead.) However, the quickest way to find your own site is by clicking <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Find embark location</span> (available when the map is zoomed out).
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Choosing_a_Good_Site">Choosing a Good Site</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Choosing a Good Site">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Choosing a decent embark site is crucial for beginners. Highly skilled players can run a fortress on an evil glacier, but for now, stick to friendly environments. Look for features in an embark site that will make your first fort easier to manage.
</p>
<table class="metadata plainlinks ambox ambox-notice" style="" role="presentation">
<tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width: 52px;"><img alt="" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="40" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text" style=""><span class="mbox-text-span">The world tooltip will only show features from the moused-over tile, but since the embark area covers multiple tiles it can contain <b>multiple biomes</b>. It is <b>very important</b> to inspect all tiles in a potential site. Each may have significantly different features such as an aquifer or evil biome <b>not initially shown</b> in the info due to not being under the cursor.<span class="hide-when-compact">  </span><span class="hide-when-compact"> </span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><br />
</p>
<div style="float: none; clear:both; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: auto; width: 80%;">
<div style="background: #00a; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Starting Site</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/0/03/DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png/350px-DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png" decoding="async" width="350" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/0/03/DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png/525px-DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/0/03/DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png/700px-DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiStartingSiteExample.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An example of a good starting location, note details in the top-right corner</div></div></div>
<p>For your first game, find a site with the following properties:
</p>
<ul><li><b>NO <a href="/index.php/Aquifer" title="Aquifer">Aquifer</a></b> (or at least no <b>heavy</b> or <b>varied</b> aquifers. Light is interesting on later embarks, but heavy guarantees <b><a href="/index.php/Fun" class="mw-redirect" title="Fun">Fun</a></b>!)</li>
<li><b>Trees:</b> Woodland or Heavily Forested (or, at the very least, sparsely forested)</li>
<li><b>Surroundings:</b> Serene, calm, or at least <b>not</b> any evil or savage biome.</li>
<li>A <b>River</b></li></ul>
<p>The following are also good to have, but focus on getting a decent site, not a perfect one.
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/index.php/Climate" title="Climate">Temperature</a>:</b> Warm or Temperate</li>
<li><b>Clay, Sand, or Soil</b> makes farming easier when starting out, also can enable pottery or glass</li>
<li><b>Flux stone layer</b> For a steel industry</li>
<li>Avoid sites containing <b>towers</b>, <b>goblins</b>, or other groups at war with you.</li>
<li>The site should be on the same land mass as an active dwarven civilization.</li></ul>
<p>See <b><a href="/index.php/Quickstart_guide/Starting_site" title="Quickstart guide/Starting site">Starting site</a></b> for more info on why these characteristics are important.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p><br />
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a href="/index.php/File:Quickstart-finder-v50.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/9/96/Quickstart-finder-v50.png/230px-Quickstart-finder-v50.png" decoding="async" width="230" height="439" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/9/96/Quickstart-finder-v50.png/345px-Quickstart-finder-v50.png 1.5x, /images/9/96/Quickstart-finder-v50.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:Quickstart-finder-v50.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Initial suggested finder criteria</div></div></div>
<p>While finding a site is not as simple as world generation, the <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Find embark location</span> button at the bottom of the screen can help. (Different buttons are shown with the map zoomed out or in; left-click will zoom in on the map, right-click will close an open menu or zoom out.)
</p><p>Once the find tool has finished searching with matches found, press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> to look at the results. Any region with a match will be indicated by a green rectangle or <span style="color: #13FD65; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">X</span>s on the map, or close partial matches by a yellow rectangle or red <span style="color: #E811FF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">X</span>s. Clicking on one of those will zoom in to show the actual sites in much the same way (partial matches are instead yellow <span style="color: #FFFFFF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">X</span>s in ASCII mode). On the zoomed in map, existing sites will be shown as red rectangles or <span style="color: #E811FF; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">░</span>s; or white rectangles or magenta <span style="color: #D79B2D; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">░</span>s for sites of the currently selected dwarven civilization if that list is open.
</p><p>The <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Choose origin civilization</span> button on the zoomed out map shows a list of the dwarven civilizations on this world. Selecting one will center the map on their capital with a blue outline on each of their sites (no outline in ASCII mode), and show population and site counts.
</p><p>Additionally, when placing the embark area you can resize it using the buttons on-screen. A 4×4 embark (the default) is usually reasonable, but you may want to change the size to avoid an undesirable biome or match your finder criteria.
</p><p>Possible causes of partial matches include:
</p>
<ul><li>"Calm" surroundings can be rare, you can try "Wilderness" instead.</li>
<li>"≤ Deep" doesn't include "very deep" soil, you can try "N/A" but make sure at least part of the site has some (it should since clay and sand count).</li>
<li>"No" Aquifer (either type) means in the entire embark area; but even if some tiles have one, others might not. If you do embark at such a site, remember which tiles don't so you can dig down there.</li></ul>
<p>You don't need a perfect site, but if you are unable to find a site that you are willing to embark on, you could always create a new world. Otherwise, move on to the next step.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Skills_and_Equipment">Skills and Equipment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Skills and Equipment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: #0a0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Optional: Preparing Carefully</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>If, at this point, you'd like to get into all of the details of picking individual skills and equipment for your expedition, select <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Prepare for the journey carefully</span> and see <b><a href="/index.php/Quickstart_guide/Preparing_carefully" title="Quickstart guide/Preparing carefully">Preparing carefully</a></b> for instructions. <b>This is completely optional</b>.
And preparing carefully makes little difference in the long run, especially without experience as to what to change.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p>Now the <b>Prepare for the Journey</b> screen should appear. You will be given the choice to either:
</p>
<ul><li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Play Now!</span></li>
<li><span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Prepare for the journey carefully</span>.</li></ul>
<p>In addition, settings are also displayed on the right-hand side.
Turn enemies to <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Off</span>. Selecting <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Play Now!</span> will start you out with a default set of equipment that is reasonably safe, allowing you to skip having to set up your skills and equipment. If you'd like to get going now, just select that option.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h1><span class="mw-headline" id="A_Minimal_Fortress">A Minimal Fortress</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: A Minimal Fortress">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h1>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/9/95/DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png/300px-DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="167" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/9/95/DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png/450px-DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/9/95/DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png/600px-DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiGettingYourBearingsExample.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Starting out. In this example, the dwarves will be digging out an entrance tunnel in the cliff on the right.</div></div></div>
<p>At this point, you have embarked, and your dwarves have arrived at their destination. You will see your dwarves clustered around their wagonful of supplies, somewhere near the center of your map. <b>Immediately hit <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Space</span></span> to pause the game</b> unless it is already paused.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Getting_your_bearings">Getting your bearings</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Getting your bearings">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>Do not unpause the game just yet.</b> Take a look around with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">w</span></span><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">a</span></span><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">s</span></span><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">d</span></span>. Look up and down a few <a href="/index.php/Z-level" title="Z-level">z-levels</a> with the scroll wheel. You can zoom in and out with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Ctrl</span></span>-scroll wheel. Place the cursor on various tiles to familiarize yourself with what the symbols mean.  If you get lost, you can press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">F1</span></span> (or <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Fn</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">F1</span></span> on some systems) to return to the wagon.  (You can define more <a href="/index.php/Hotkeys" title="Hotkeys">hotkeys</a> later, to jump quickly to other sites of interest.) Notice the terrain features, the vegetation, and any minerals visible. If you chose a site with flowing water, where is it? What about pools of water? The more carefully you examine your site before breaking ground, the better off you will be.
</p><p>In the bottom left, click the citizens information button to see a list of your dwarves. In the <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Others</span> tab, you can see any wild animals that may be nearby.
</p><p>The <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Stocks</span> button at the top of the screen will show the items owned by your fortress.
</p><p>On the left, there are buttons for various message logs.
</p><p>Your wagon serves as the initial meeting area for your dwarves. Since you should have started in a non-freezing, calm (low savagery), non-evil biome, you shouldn't face any immediate danger, but if for some reason the area around your wagon proves to be unsafe, immediately designate another meeting zone (see <a href="#Temporary_Meeting_Area">Temporary Meeting Area</a> below).
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Controlling_Your_Dwarves">Controlling Your Dwarves</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Controlling Your Dwarves">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The first thing to keep in mind is that, for the most part, you can't directly control your dwarves the way you control characters in a typical fantasy RPG. Instead, you <b>designate</b> things that need to be done and then dwarves with the appropriate labor assignments will decide what to do. 
</p><p>Some tasks receive a higher priority. For example, if a dwarf needs to eat, then he will go eat, and only get around to digging a tunnel once he is done eating. It is also possible to designate things that no dwarf is able to do. For example, if you designate an area to mine, but no dwarf has mining as one of his allowed labors, or no dwarf has a <a href="/index.php/Pick" title="Pick">pick</a>, then the mining will never get done, and the game will not always advise you of why.
</p><p>So, what you are doing throughout the game is essentially giving your dwarves a detailed group-wide to-do list, but it's up to them to figure out which one of them will execute any given task if the task is even possible. Often many of the details of how a task is performed (such as exactly which rock will be used to make crafts) are left up to them.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Labor_and_work_details">Labor and work details</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Labor and work details">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: #aa0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Utilities</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>You may have noticed that the UI for managing dwarves is a bit difficult to use. There are a few utilities available for this purpose (for Windows, Mac OS X, and most Linux systems): 
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/index.php/Utilities#Dwarf_Therapist" title="Utilities">Dwarf Therapist</a></b> can make labor management considerably easier, especially when you're dealing with twenty times the number of dwarves you have now. It can group and sort dwarves by multiple attributes and display their preferences, mood, and more.</li>
<li><b><a href="/index.php/Utility:DFHack" title="Utility:DFHack">DFHack</a></b> includes "Dwarf Manipulator", a UI for managing labors. It has fewer features than Dwarf Therapist, but displays much of the same information and is adequate for normal use. In addition, it is accessible from within DF via <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">u</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">l</span></span>, eliminating the need to constantly switch between applications.</li></ul>
</div>
</div>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint relarticle mainarticle"><i>Main article: <a href="/index.php/Labor" title="Labor">Labor</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p><b>Labors</b> are how you control what types of tasks a dwarf is allowed to do. When dwarves are idle, it could be because you haven't given them anything to do, or it could be because none of the idle dwarves have been told that they're allowed to do the types of tasks you've designated. For example, if you designate an area to mine, but none of the dwarves have the mining labor enabled, they will all just sit around ignoring your mining designation, thinking that it isn't their job.
</p><p>Labors are assigned to dwarves in groups called <b>work details</b>. Open the labor menu from the bottom left to see all the default work details and their assignments.
</p><p>Fortunately, you don't need to assign a dwarf for every single labor in the game; work details can be set to "everybody does this" to allow any idle dwarf to pick up the job.
</p><p><b>While you're here</b>, set the Hunters and Fisherdwarves work details to "nobody does this." Dwarves with these details enabled will constantly be outside attempting to perform them, and for now you don't want dwarves wandering around alone where they can get killed (in addition, they won't be doing anything useful, like hauling).
</p><p>Also, the default embark comes with three pickaxes: so for efficiency, make sure two dwarves have the Miners detail enabled.
</p><p>As dwarves perform jobs, they gain skill in those areas which leads to them working faster or producing higher-quality things. Note that <i>any</i> unskilled dwarf can perform any labor given the necessary equipment and materials; they'll just be worse at it.
</p><p>The default work details contain all the essential labors for the very start of your fortress, but this guide will involve other labors. Keep in mind that at some point you'll have to assign the following labors by creating custom work details:
</p>
<table class="wikitable">

</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>Jewelry</td>
<td>Gem Cutting
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span id="Strike_The_Earth!"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Strike_The_Earth.21">Strike The Earth!</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Strike The Earth!">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: green; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Getting your dwarves to safety</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>As you now know, you can't control your dwarves directly. So how do you tell them to get inside your newly dug rooms?
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/index.php/Activity_zone#Meeting_area" class="mw-redirect" title="Activity zone">Meeting Area</a> You can designate a Meeting Area zone inside the new rooms. Press <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_z.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui z.png" src="/images/1/13/Ui_z.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="35" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span></span></span></span> and click "Meeting Area". Draw a rectangle to create a meeting area, then click "Accept". <i>See also the <a href="/index.php/Zone" class="mw-redirect" title="Zone">zone</a> page for more information.</i></li>
<li><a href="/index.php/Stockpiles" class="mw-redirect" title="Stockpiles">Stockpiles</a> (see <a href="/index.php/Quickstart_guide#Stockpiles" title="Quickstart guide">below</a>) Stockpiles tell your dwarves where to put things. Create a stockpile for everything, and dwarves will start to haul all your items there.</li></ul>
</div>
</div>
<p>Decide where you will build your main entrance. Generally, you will want to get all your dwarves and supplies inside a protected area as quickly as possible. The best strategy is to put the entrance near your wagon to speed up the process of hauling all of your supplies inside.
</p><p>The digging orders menu allows you to select areas to dig. Click the pick axe at the bottom or press <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_m.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui m.png" src="/images/d/d7/Ui_m.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span></span></span></span>. There are multiple methods of digging:
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/index.php/Mining" title="Mining">Mining</a></b> (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span>) removes solid, floor-to-ceiling terrain (natural 'walls') on the z-level selected, leaving behind a rock or soil surface (also referred to as a natural floor). This does <b>not</b> do anything in areas without natural walls (for example, the surface or previously-mined areas).</li>
<li><b><a href="/index.php/Channel" title="Channel">Channeling</a></b> (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span>-<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">u</span></span>) removes <i>natural</i> (rock/soil) floors (either created naturally or by mining) and creates a ramp (▲) on the z-level below. Note that you will see a down arrow (▼) on the current z-level, indicating a ramp on the level below. (For best results, ensure that the area below is unrevealed, i.e. black).</li></ul>
<p>To designate an area for digging:
</p>
<ol><li>Hit <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span> to bring up the digging orders menu.</li>
<li>Hit <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span> to mine or <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">u</span></span> to channel (see above)</li>
<li>Draw a rectangular square that you want to dig out.</li>
<li>A rectangle will be highlighted and a miner will start to dig out this area once you unpause the game with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Space</span></span>.</li></ol>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:227px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/d/d1/DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png/225px-DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png" decoding="async" width="225" height="346" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/d/d1/DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png/338px-DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/d/d1/DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png/450px-DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiDigChannelDifference.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Demonstrating the difference between mining and channeling. Mining creates empty space on the same level where it is designated. Channeling creates empty space in the level below, clearing the floor. The levels are connected by up/down ramps.</div></div></div>
<div style="float: left; clear:left; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-left:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: red; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Channeling</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>Note that channeling can be <a href="/index.php/Fun" class="mw-redirect" title="Fun">dangerous</a>. Unless you know what you're doing, you should only ever make a pit one z-level deep. If you dig a pit multiple z-levels deep, only the lowest level will have an upward <a href="/index.php/Ramp" title="Ramp">ramp</a>, which is not enough for dwarves to leave the pit. (Dwarves can <a href="/index.php/Climb" class="mw-redirect" title="Climb">climb</a> out in some circumstances, but this is unreliable.) 
</p>
<div class="dfdiagram" style="">

color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ff0000; background-color:#000000;">▼</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ff0000; background-color:#000000;">▲</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td></tr>
	<tr><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; 	<tr><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block;
