color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffff00; background-color:#ff0000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td></tr>
</tbody></table></div>
</div>
<p>This diagram shows the cross-section (side view) of 1×1 pits channeled 1 z-level deep, 2 z-levels deep and the correct way to do a 2 z-level deep ramp. The appearance of "downward ramps" can be confusing as there is no such thing - the down arrow indicates a ramp on the level below. Dwarves in the first pit can walk up the ramp to ground level and escape, while dwarves in the second pit cannot use the ramp at all. The third pit lets dwarves walk back to the surface again since the two ramps are offset to produce a continued slope. In short, channels (particularly channels multiple z-levels deep) can be dangerous. Digging an entryway from the surface level is one of the few times you'll ever need to channel.
</p><p><small>Stairs can also be used for an entryway, but channels allow <a href="/index.php/Wagon" title="Wagon">wagons</a> entry to your fortress.</small>
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p>If your wagon is near a <a href="/index.php/Cliff" title="Cliff">cliff</a> or hill (generally speaking, any difference in levels, usually shown by the existence of natural ramps), you can just designate a tunnel to mine (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span>) into the cliff to create an entryway. If the wagon is surrounded by flat terrain, <a href="/index.php/Channel" title="Channel">channel</a> out a 3×3 rectangle on the surface with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span>-<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">u</span></span> to create a sort of pit with ramps on the edges, then go down one z-level with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">c</span></span> (or use the mouse scroll wheel) and tunnel into one wall of the pit (with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span>) to create your entry.
</p><p>Dig a hallway one tile wide and <i>at least</i> 10 long, ideally more like 20. This will be your entryway.
</p><p>Your entryway defines the boundary between your safe and protected inner fort, and the big, bad, outside world. You want this to be your only entrance, so that you only have to worry about defending this one opening. A somewhat-outdated video guide to starting a fortress can be found <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CLYDcuk29bE&amp;feature=plcp">here</a>. (Note that this applies to v0.34.11, not v50.14, so some parts may be inaccurate in the current version.)
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Additional_miners"><i>Additional miners</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Additional miners">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Mining will go faster if you have more than one dwarf doing it. By default, only one dwarf has the Mining labor enabled, but this can be changed fairly easily:
</p>
<ul><li>Press <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_y.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui y.png" src="/images/c/cb/Ui_y.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="36" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">y</span></span></span></span></span> to open the labor menu, and select "Miners" on the left side.</li>
<li>Choose a dwarf that isn't doing anything especially useful (the fish cleaner is a good choice for a beginning fortress, but you can always change your mind if you end up with a useless peasant later on)</li>
<li>Click the check box next to the dwarf to enable the mining labor.</li>
<li>Exit with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> or right mouse.</li></ul>
<p>The next time you designate an area for mining, both of your miners should start working (assuming they're not busy doing something else).
</p><p><b>Notes:</b>
</p>
<ul><li>Each miner requires a <a href="/index.php/Pick" title="Pick">pick</a>. A standard embark comes with 3 picks. If you want more than three miners, you'll need to forge more picks (forging is covered later in this guide). Two miners should be adequate for most fortresses, but more miners can add reliability (for when a miner decides to sleep) and speed. For now, you'll almost never need more than two miners, but you'll want more once your fortress expands.</li>
<li>If you're digging a one-tile-wide hallway, only one miner can work from an end.</li>
<li>Mining, Wood Cutting, &amp; Hunting labors are mutually exclusive - a dwarf can only have up to one of these professions active at a time. For this reason, it's not recommended to make your only woodcutter a miner, since they won't be able to cut wood anymore.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Delving_Secure_Lodgings">Delving Secure Lodgings</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Delving Secure Lodgings">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Near the middle of the entry tunnel, build a 5×5 room, and link it to the entrance tunnel with a 3-tile-wide passageway. Expand the main entry tunnel to <i>three</i> tiles wide from the entrance of the new room to the outside entry. At the end of the entry tunnel, dig a small room, which will later become your main stairwell. Two tiles past that, dig a larger room, which will later become your general stockpile, and connect it to the stairwell with a narrow passageway.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiExampleLayout.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/2/26/DFwikiExampleLayout.png/300px-DFwikiExampleLayout.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/2/26/DFwikiExampleLayout.png/450px-DFwikiExampleLayout.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/2/26/DFwikiExampleLayout.png/600px-DFwikiExampleLayout.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiExampleLayout.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An example layout, as described in this section. Note the 3-tile wide passage - this allows merchants to access your depot room. Note that the turn also needs to be 3 tiles wide; otherwise, wagons won't be able to access the room.</div></div></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Room_dimensions"><i>Room dimensions</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Room dimensions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Apart from wagon access (3 tiles wide), the trade depot (5×5), and other workshops (3×3), there are no fixed dimensions you need to worry about. The lower limiting factor is the traffic your tunnels receive (dwarves may have to start climbing over each other), and the space your rooms need (stockpiles, tables/chairs, livestock). The practical maximum size is limited by how long it takes your miners to dig the rooms out, especially if they're digging in stone instead of soil (digging through soil is much faster). Most sites have at least one level soil layer below ground level, which is where you're digging right now, but as you dig deeper you'll hit stone (if you haven't already), and digging will become slower. In most fortresses, even the main hallways never need to be wider than 3 tiles, and needing more than 3 tiles of stairs per floor is very rare. A 3×3 per floor staircase (9 stairs!) is absolute overkill for anything but 20-year-old 300-resident capitals. For most tunnels in your fortress, 2 tiles wide will be sufficient, and many will be fine at just 1 tile wide. 11×11 is a reasonable size for stockpile rooms. However, something smaller is perfectly fine for rarer stockpiles, offices, and small dining rooms. Commoners’ bedrooms need not be larger than the amount of furniture you want inside.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mining_safety"><i>Mining safety</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Mining safety">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>While mining, take care to avoid digging into <a href="/index.php/Water" title="Water">water</a>. Dwarves are usually poor swimmers, and are unlikely to escape from an underground flood. However, it is safe to mine <i>next to</i> underground water, as long as you leave at least one "wall" tile between them (see the picture to the right). You can also mine one z-level under a body of water (for example, mining under a river), but you will have to designate each tile individually because DF automatically cancels digging of newly-revealed "damp" tiles (tiles are considered damp when they are adjacent to a water tile, regardless of whether the water tile is on the same z-level or not).
</p><p>Also note that <b>water can flow diagonally</b>:
</p>
<div class="dfdiagram" style="">
<div class="dfdiagram-frame">

	<tbody><tr><td><span style="display:block; color:#00f; background-color:#000000;">≈</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">.</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#00f; background-color:#000000;">≈</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">.</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td></tr>
	<tr><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">.</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">.</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">.</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">▓</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td></tr>
	<tr><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td><td><span style="display:block; color:#ffffff; background-color:#000000;">&#160;</span></td></tr>

</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Stockpiles"><i>Stockpiles</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Stockpiles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiStockpileMenu.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/0/00/DFwikiStockpileMenu.png/300px-DFwikiStockpileMenu.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="443" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/0/00/DFwikiStockpileMenu.png 1.5x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiStockpileMenu.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Keep corpses, refuse, stone and wood out of general use stockpiles. You can come back and change the settings on this stockpile by clicking on it to open the stockpile menu, and clicking "Custom". Try to remember to come back here to disable/forbid types of things as you create more specific stockpiles for them.</div></div></div>
<p><b>Stockpiles</b> are very important. These areas are where your dwarves will drop things for storage when they aren't needed elsewhere. To create a <b>general purpose stockpile</b> for your first storage area:
</p>
<ol><li>Hit <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_p.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui p.png" src="/images/4/4a/Ui_p.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span></span></span></span> to open the Stockpiles menu.</li>
<li>Click the plus sign at the bottom to add a new stockpile.</li>
<li>Draw a rectangle and click "Accept".</li>
<li>Click <a href="/index.php/Stockpile#Custom_stockpiles" title="Stockpile">"Custom"</a> to change the goods that the stockpile accepts. Enable everything but <b>Corpses</b>, <b>Refuse</b>, <b>Stone</b>, <b>Gems</b>, and <b>Wood</b>. To do this, first click "All" in the top left to enable everything, then go through each type you want to exclude, and click "None" in the top-center of the screen. This will reject all goods of that type.</li>
<li><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> or right mouse twice to exit the stockpiles menu.</li></ol>
<p>Once you exit the stockpiles menu and unpause, you should see dwarves running off to haul everything from your wagon into the new stockpile area. Later, if you like, you can change what sort of things the stockpile accepts by hitting <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span>, clicking on the stockpile, then changing the stockpile settings as above.
</p><p>It is particularly important to <b>keep wood, stone, refuse, and corpses out of your general purpose stockpile</b>, so you may want to double check to make sure all of these things are disabled in the stockpile settings. Failure to keep these things out of this stockpile will rapidly fill it up, causing workshops to become cluttered when dwarves can't store things in the stockpile.
<b>Note:</b> When assigning stockpiles, you should make sure they're in a vacant area (i.e. the tiles should not have any items already stored on them). Dwarves will not haul items to occupied tiles, so make sure the area is vacant (and already mined out) before assigning a stockpile.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Stairways"><i>Stairways</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Stairways">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 45%;">
<div style="background: #0a0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Up, Down, Up/Down: Types of Stairs</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>In Dwarf Fortress, every <a href="/index.php/Z-level" title="Z-level">z-level</a> is composed of a <a href="/index.php/Floor" title="Floor">floor</a> and a <a href="/index.php/Wall" title="Wall">wall</a> (or "space between floors"). The confusingly named "down" and "up" <a href="/index.php/Stairs" title="Stairs">stairs</a> have nothing to do with the direction creatures can move to; instead, down stairs penetrate floors, while up stairs penetrate walls. Up/down stairs penetrate the wall and the floor below. <i>(note the picture to the left)</i>
</p><p>When you designate a staircase to be dug out, the top level will be down-stairs, any inner levels will be up/down stairs, and the bottom level will be up-stairs.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p><br />
Dig a <a href="/index.php/Stairs" title="Stairs">stairway</a> in the room you dug out for the stairwell (<i>not</i> the 5×5 room that you dug out earlier): press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span>, click on the floor of the room to start the staircase, scroll down one level, and click again to finish designating the staircase. This will create down-stairs on the top level, and up-stairs on the level below. To continue digging downwards later, you can designate another staircase (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span>) starting on the lowest exposed level and continuing downwards. For now just dig down one level.
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:602px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DF2014_Terraform.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/4/4d/DF2014_Terraform.png/600px-DF2014_Terraform.png" decoding="async" width="600" height="295" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/4/4d/DF2014_Terraform.png 1.5x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DF2014_Terraform.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>This is how the different stairs would look like from the side.</i></div></div></div>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Temporary_Meeting_Area">Temporary Meeting Area</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Temporary Meeting Area">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/1/10/DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png/300px-DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="102" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/1/10/DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png/450px-DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/1/10/DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png/600px-DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiTemporaryMeetingHallExample.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An example meeting area. Note that this layer has a different type of soil than the layer above - this can happen often. Also note that the "north" side of this room is directly below the lake in the level above, but no water is present.</div></div></div>
<p>On the second z-level below ground (the one below the stockpile level, which you just reached with the staircase), dig a short, 3-tile wide passageway (this only needs to be 1-2 tiles long). Past that, dig out a room between 5×5 and 7×7, leaving room to enlarge it in at least one direction in the future. Using the <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_z.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui z.png" src="/images/1/13/Ui_z.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="35" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span></span></span></span> key, create a meeting area in the room you just created, filling the entire room (be careful not to make this too small lest your <a href="/index.php/Overcrowding" title="Overcrowding">overcrowded</a> animals start fighting). This works much like creating a stockpile except that you define what the area is for before you draw the rectangle. Select "Meeting area", draw the rectangle, filling the entire room, and click "Accept". Your idle dwarves will hang around in this area, hopefully keeping them inside the fort and out of trouble. 
</p><p>NOTE: Again, make sure your <a href="/index.php/Zones" title="Zones">activity zone</a> is already mined out before attempting to designate the meeting area.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Refuse">Refuse</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Refuse">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/6/61/Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg/300px-Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg" decoding="async" width="300" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/6/61/Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg/450px-Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg 1.5x, /images/thumb/6/61/Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg/600px-Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:Dwarf_fort_tut_miasma.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Avoiding <a href="/index.php/Miasma" title="Miasma">Miasma</a></div></div></div>
<p>Outside your fort entrance, use <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_p.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui p.png" src="/images/4/4a/Ui_p.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span></span></span></span> and click the "plus stockpile" icon to create a stock<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span>ile for <a href="/index.php/Stockpile#Refuse" title="Stockpile">refuse</a> (trash can icon) <i>at least</i> 5×5 in size. This should be outside in the open or you will have problems with <a href="/index.php/Miasma" title="Miasma">Miasma</a>. If you do not disable <a href="/index.php/Vermin" title="Vermin">vermin</a> (Item Types -&gt; remains), you will probably have to expand it later as it will fill up with vermin remains rather quickly. If you are seeing refuse appear in your general-purpose stockpile instead of the refuse pile, click on the general stockpile and check its custom settings to make sure refuse has been disabled.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Food">Food</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Food">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Food is necessary for your dwarves' survival -  to keep functioning, they require constant supplies of food and drink - the amount of food and drink currently available is displayed in the status bar at the top of the screen. Luckily, your dwarves will eat almost everything raw, including plants.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Farming"><i>Farming</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Farming">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>For a reliable, long-term food and alcohol supply, you'll need to set up a farm. Dig out a medium-sized room in a <a href="/index.php/Soil" title="Soil">soil</a> layer (including sand, clay, loam, silt, peat, and ooze) accessible from inside your existing fortress. 5×5 is a good size to start with, but you'll want to leave room to expand in at least one direction. You must pick an <i>underground</i> area with mud or soil*. Placing this near the stockpiles is more efficient, since farmers won't need to travel as far.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:150px;"><div class="mw-collapsible" id="mw-customcollapsible-classicimage"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwiki5by53by3farm.png" class="image"><img alt="DFwiki5by53by3farm.png" src="/images/thumb/6/6e/DFwiki5by53by3farm.png/150px-DFwiki5by53by3farm.png" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" srcset="/images/thumb/6/6e/DFwiki5by53by3farm.png/225px-DFwiki5by53by3farm.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/6/6e/DFwiki5by53by3farm.png/300px-DFwiki5by53by3farm.png 2x" /></a></div><div class="mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" id="mw-customcollapsible-classicimage"><a href="/index.php/File:Quickstart_layout_3.png" class="image"><img alt="Quickstart layout 3.png" src="/images/b/bd/Quickstart_layout_3.png" decoding="async" width="150" height="214" /></a></div><div class="thumbcaption"><span class="mw-customtoggle-classicimage mw-ui-button mw-ui-progressive" style="float:right; padding:0px; user-select: none;">Toggle</span>A 5×5 room with a 3×3 farm plot</div></div></div>
<p><sub>* Hopefully you have chosen a site with a soil layer, which will make farming much easier, but if not you will need to <a href="/index.php/Irrigation" title="Irrigation">irrigate</a> to create the required mud on stone floors.</sub>
</p><p>Use <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bo.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bo.png" src="/images/a/aa/Ui_bo.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">o</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bof.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bof.png" src="/images/0/0a/Ui_bof.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">f</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bofp.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bofp.png" src="/images/4/45/Ui_bofp.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span></span></span></span> to build a 3×3 <a href="/index.php/Farming" title="Farming">farm plot</a> in the room you just created. Position the farm plot ideally near the wall to leave space for more plots later on.
</p><p>The <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Planters</span> work detail must be enabled for at least one dwarf, or the farm plot won't get built and farming will not take place. By default, Planters is set to "Everybody does this", so there's no need to change this now.
</p><p><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">Esc</span></span> out of the build menu and wait for the farmer dwarf to create the plot. Once the plot is built, click on it, and set the plot to grow <a href="/index.php/Plump_helmet" title="Plump helmet">plump helmets</a> during all seasons. You need to go through each season tab to enable plump helmets in all seasons &#8212; otherwise you'll end up with an idle field for 3/4ths of the year.
</p><p>Later, if you are curious what is planted in each plot this season and how much, click on the plot and it will show the list of seeds currently planted. There is no icon for a partially grown plant, so an empty field will look identical to a fully planted field until your crops are ready for harvest.
</p><p>Note that a default embark starts with <i>five</i> plump helmet seeds &#8212; for now, only half of your field will end up being planted. Eventually, as your dwarves consume plump helmets, more seeds will become available and will be automatically planted by an unoccupied farmer.
</p>
<dl><dd><i>For more troubleshooting tips, see <a href="/index.php/How_do_I_build_a_farm" class="mw-redirect" title="How do I build a farm">How do I build a farm</a></i></dd></dl>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Emergency_food_sources"><i>Emergency food sources</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Emergency food sources">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Occasionally, even with a working plump helmet farm, you may experience food shortages. For now, you should have plenty of food on hand left over from embarking. However, if you ever run low on food, there are a few ways to obtain more:
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Plant_gathering"><i>Plant gathering</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Plant gathering">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>If you have shrubs (<span style="color: #A2DC34; background: #000000; font-size: 135%; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, &#39;Quicktype Mono&#39;, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Lucida Console&#39;, &#39;Lucida Sans Typewriter&#39;, monospace; font-weight:bold; padding: 0; line-height: 1;">"</span>) growing above ground, you can harvest plants from them. Note that this requires a dwarf with the <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Plant gatherers</span> work detail, and time (this can take a while for an inexperienced dwarf, and it doesn't always yield edible plants). To start, <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">g</span></span>ather plants on the surface (similar to selecting an area for mining, except it only selects plants in the given rectangle). Once processed, some will leave behind harvested plants (often edible berries).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Butchering"><i>Butchering</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Butchering">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>If you suddenly run low on food, butchering an animal is another option. Build a <a href="/index.php/Butcher" title="Butcher">butcher</a> shop <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bo.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bo.png" src="/images/a/aa/Ui_bo.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">o</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bof.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bof.png" src="/images/0/0a/Ui_bof.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">f</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bofb.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bofb.png" src="/images/2/21/Ui_bofb.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span></span> and mark one of your animals for slaughtering (press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">u</span></span>, click on "Pets/Livestock", and click the meat cleaver next to the animal you want to slaughter). A dwarf with the butchering labor enabled will haul the animal off to the butcher's shop, work for a while, and produce neat stacks of meat products.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Building_material">Building material</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Building material">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Initially, <a href="/index.php/Wood" title="Wood">wood</a> is probably a good choice for building material, as it's lightweight and can be easily obtained. You will need plenty of building materials as your fortress grows, but wood will suffice for now. If you are unable to locate enough wood (or if you run out of trees, which is unlikely at this point), extend your staircase down to a stone level (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span></span>-<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span>) and mine out a small area (at least 5×5) to obtain stone.
</p><p>Even if you don't have trees, you can obtain 3 logs from your embark wagon. Click on your wagon, and click the button in the top right to deconstruct it. This will flag the wagon for disassembly. Eventually a carpenter will come along and turn the useless wagon into 3 units of wood. (Removing other buildings is done the same way.)
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Woodcutting"><i>Woodcutting</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Woodcutting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Assuming your site has <a href="/index.php/Tree" title="Tree">trees</a> above ground, now is a good time to start obtaining wood. Create a stock<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span>ile for wood outside your entrance (preferably near to it). As it will only be temporary, don't make it too big (maybe 5×3, or 15 tiles total). Later, you will move this closer to your carpenter's workshop (once you build one with <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bo.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bo.png" src="/images/a/aa/Ui_bo.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">o</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bop.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bop.png" src="/images/8/86/Ui_bop.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span></span></span></span>), so don't worry about placement too much. Also near the entry, designate a couple of trees to be chopped down with <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_l.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui l.png" src="/images/b/b2/Ui_l.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">l</span></span></span></span></span>. One tree will produce many logs, so only designate three to five at this point. If you designate too many trees, your woodcutters will spend all of their time chopping them down and hauling the resulting logs, instead of doing other work. As soon as one tree is cut down and its wood stored in a stockpile, you can proceed to the next step (your woodcutter will continue cutting down any remaining designated trees).
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Drinks">Drinks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Drinks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Drinks can be more problematic than food, since they require more preparation (except for <a href="/index.php/Water" title="Water">water</a>, that is). In warmer weather, you can specify a "water source" activity <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span>one around a lake or river on the surface to keep your dwarves from dying of thirst, but dwarves deprived of <a href="/index.php/Alcohol" title="Alcohol">alcohol</a> slow down and become unhappy. In addition, drinking outside can be dangerous &#8212; dwarves running outside constantly risk running into wild animals, or worse. Creating a <a href="/index.php/Still" title="Still">still</a> to brew alcohol is the simplest solution to these problems.
</p><p>You need a brewer to brew drinks. Fortunately, the brewing labor is enabled on all dwarves by default. If you want to change this later, use the <a href="/index.php/Labor" title="Labor">labor menu</a> (<span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_y.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui y.png" src="/images/c/cb/Ui_y.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="36" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">y</span></span></span></span></span>).
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiCompletedStillQuickstart.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/9/9c/DFwikiCompletedStillQuickstart.png/300px-DFwikiCompletedStillQuickstart.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="205" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/9/9c/DFwikiCompletedStillQuickstart.png 1.5x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiCompletedStillQuickstart.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A completed still</div></div></div>
<p>Assuming you have building materials available (which you will if your woodcutter has been doing their job), you can now create a still:
</p>
<ol><li>Dig out a 3×3 area connected to the farm plot.</li>
<li>Use <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bo.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bo.png" src="/images/a/aa/Ui_bo.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">o</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bof.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bof.png" src="/images/0/0a/Ui_bof.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">f</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bofl.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bofl.png" src="/images/b/b8/Ui_bofl.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">l</span></span></span></span></span> to build a still. Position it in the 3×3 area you just created.</li>
<li>Click on a building material for the still (this is probably one of the logs you just cut down by default).</li></ol>
<p>After a short delay, one of your dwarves should run off, drag a log over to the workshop site, and build the workshop. (This is also how building other workshops works, but you won't need to do that yet).
</p><p>To brew drinks, click on the still, click "Add new task", and "Brew drink from plant". <b>This will not work yet</b>, since you don't have any empty barrels or rock pots, but you should start brewing in the first six months (see <a href="/index.php/Calendar" title="Calendar">Calendar</a> and <a href="/index.php/Status" title="Status">Status</a>).
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Pasture">Pasture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Pasture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: #0a0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Grazers</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>If you aren't sure whether or not an animal is a grazer, you can check <a href="/index.php/Category:Grazer" title="Category:Grazer">this category</a>. (You can also <a href="/index.php/Special:Search" title="Special:Search">search</a> for the animal on this wiki.)
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p>If you have any grazing animals with you, such as the draft animals used to pull your wagon, they will die if they are kept away from grass for too long. Use <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_z.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui z.png" src="/images/1/13/Ui_z.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="35" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span></span></span></span> to create a Pen/<a href="/index.php/Pasture" title="Pasture">Pasture</a> zone over a grassy area outside and assign your grazing animals to it with the "plus bunny" icon in the top right of the zone menu. This area needs to be about 10×10 or so to ensure they have enough grass and don't trample it all. The amount of grass required varies greatly, depending on the type(s) of animals being pastured.  If you intend to keep grazing animals permanently, you may need vastly larger pastures later.  As an alternative, you might wish to <a href="/index.php/Butcher%27s_shop" title="Butcher&#39;s shop">slaughter</a> your largest animals for food and materials.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Designing_your_first_fortress">Designing your first fortress</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Designing your first fortress">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>While this guide recommends a vertical fortress design around a central stairwell, with each z-level being used for a particular purpose, it is not really that important to use this design for your first fortress. Therefore, feel free to put any of the areas described in the rest of this guide on your main level or wherever you want as long as dwarves can get to them without going outside the fort. In other words, you can think of the "levels" described in the guide more as areas that can really all be on the same level if you have space. Later you can ponder over what makes things most efficient, but for now just do whatever you find easiest. Note that you may need to dig down a bit to get to stone if you have more than one z-level of sand/clay/soil below the surface.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Workshops">Workshops</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Workshops">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/e/e2/DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png/300px-DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="258" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/e/e2/DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png/450px-DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/e/e2/DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png/600px-DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiStockpileWorkshopQuickstart.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An example workshop layout. The gem stockpile (empty) is north of the Jeweler's workshop (southwest corner), the wood stockpile is west of the Carpenter's workshop (northeast corner), and the stone stockpile occupies the rest of the space. Note the wheelbarrow in the stone stockpile.</div></div></div>
<p>Most labors of your dwarves need a place where they can process raw materials &#8212; <a href="/index.php/Workshop" title="Workshop">workshops</a>. Almost all of them occupy a 3×3 square, and most of them require just 1 unit of any building material (wood, stone, metal). Dig your stairwell down one level (with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">m</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span>), if you haven't already. It's fine if this layer is soil &#8212; in fact, soil is better, since it's easier to dig through (if you only have one soil layer, you can put these workshops somewhere on your first level). Dig space for your workshops off of the stairwell. It will hold your <a href="/index.php/Mechanic%27s_workshop" title="Mechanic&#39;s workshop">mechanic's</a>, <a href="/index.php/Stoneworker%27s_workshop" title="Stoneworker&#39;s workshop">stoneworker's</a>, <a href="/index.php/Carpenter%27s_workshop" title="Carpenter&#39;s workshop">carpenter's</a>, and <a href="/index.php/Jeweler%27s_workshop" title="Jeweler&#39;s workshop">jeweler's</a> <a href="/index.php/Workshop" title="Workshop">workshops</a>.
