Something to consider is stockpile proximity: the farther away the material is the dwarves use, the more time they waste with walking. So for now, dig out some more space for stockpiles close to where your new workshops will be (wood for your carpenter, stone for your stoneworker and mechanic, and gems for your jeweler).
It doesn't matter if you put everything in one large room or dig out small rooms for each workshop and stockpile. Once you've dug out your rooms, set your miners to work by adding a z-level or two to the staircase. Hopefully you'll obtain some stone by doing this, which will be useful eventually. While your miners are busy, use <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bo.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bo.png" src="/images/a/aa/Ui_bo.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">o</span></span></span></span></span> to build the workshops, using whatever building material you have. If you are still digging in soil and don't have stone yet, just use wood; the material really doesn't matter in this case. Be sure that your craftsdwarves still have labors corresponding to each workshop enabled (see <a href="#Labor_and_work_details">Labor and work details</a> above) so they will begin construction. (Dwarves already busy mining or hauling may not immediately stop to construct workshops; if you like, you may temporarily disable other labors in order to jumpstart workshop construction.) If the construction of any building gets "suspended" click on the workshop and click "Resume construction" to unsuspend it. (This can happen if another dwarf or object is blocking the way. See <a href="#.22Garbage.22_Dumping">Garbage Dumping</a> below if you find you need to remove an object.)
</p>
<div style="float: right; clear:right; border: 2px solid black; background: white; margin: 1em; margin-right:0em; width: 35%;">
<div style="background: #0a0; padding: 0.3em 0.5em; border-bottom: 1px solid black; text-align: center; font-size:120%; color:#ffffff"><b>Too Good for Menial Peon Work</b></div>
<div style="padding: 0 0.5em;">
<p>Certain labors are crucial in setting up a fort. At some point you may want to disable less important labors such as hauling for dwarves with the crucial skills of mining, masonry, architecture, carpentry, mechanics, and maybe others. You want these dwarves working on creating beds, doors, and trap components before hauling stone and cleaning.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<p><br />
Click on your stoneworker's shop and queue up one <a href="/index.php/Table" title="Table">table</a> and one <a href="/index.php/Throne" title="Throne">throne</a>/chair. You will find out why you need these in a second, but now is a good time to start building them. If you still don't have any stone at this point just use wood at the carpenter's workshop.
</p><p>At this point, it is a good idea to build a few <a href="/index.php/Wheelbarrow" title="Wheelbarrow">wheelbarrows</a> to make hauling large objects (particularly stone) more efficient. Queue up 2 or 3 at the carpenter's workshop. (Wheelbarrows are located near the bottom of the list, you will need to scroll all the way down.) While the wheelbarrows are being built, click on your stone stockpile and click the barrel icon, and increase "Max wheelbarrows" to 3. Your dwarves will automatically move wheelbarrows to the stockpile once they are built.
</p>
<h3><span id="&quot;Where_did_I_build_that_?&quot;"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".22Where_did_I_build_that_.3F.22"><i>"Where did I build that ____?"</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: &quot;Where did I build that ?&quot;">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As you build workshops, furnaces, Trade Depot, other buildings, rooms and even zones, you may start to lose track of where they all are -- or where they're supposed to be built, but some dwarf is too busy eating/drinking/hauling. There are a couple of commands available from the main UI that will help you locate what you built.
</p>
<ul><li>You can View <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_P.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui P.png" src="/images/c/c5/Ui_P.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="36" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-p">P</span></span></span></span></span> (Places) and click the "Workshops" tab to see a Building List, and also Zoom to the building/item, or view the building's tasks.</li></ul>
<ul><li>For incomplete buildings/constructions, you can also open the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">t</span></span>ask list and then recenter on the partially constructed building to find the intended location.</li></ul>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brewing">Brewing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Brewing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>You'll need <a href="/index.php/Barrel" title="Barrel">barrels</a> to store drinks for your dwarves. Queue up two or three barrels in your carpenter's workshop. (If you run out of wood at any point, cut down another tree or two outside). If a lack of wood cancelled a job, you will need to queue the job again. Go back to your still and order some drinks to be brewed. Each drink requires one barrel and one edible plant, such as a plump helmet. Even if none of yours have been harvested yet, you should have some left over from embark. Also, brewing plump helmets creates <i>two</i> seeds from one plant, which makes plump helmets an excellent choice for a beginning fortress. Five barrels should be plenty for now (each plant makes 5 "units", or servings, of booze, and dwarves don't need to drink too often, so 30 units should last you a whole year. When the stocks get low, you'll probably want to start queueing up more drinks to be made (you should have more empty barrels by then)).
</p>
<h2><span id="&quot;Garbage&quot;_Dumping"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".22Garbage.22_Dumping">"Garbage" Dumping</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: &quot;Garbage&quot; Dumping">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint relarticle mainarticle"><i>Main article: <a href="/index.php/Garbage_dump" title="Garbage dump">Garbage dump</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p><b>Note that garbage is not the same thing as refuse.</b> <a href="/index.php/Stockpile#Refuse" title="Stockpile">Refuse</a> is <a href="/index.php/Miasma" title="Miasma">rotting stuff</a>. Garbage is anything you designate to be hauled to a <a href="/index.php/Activity_zone#Garbage_Dump" class="mw-redirect" title="Activity zone">garbage dump</a>, even important things that aren't really garbage. Think of your garbage dump zone as a way to specify that objects you select will be brought to a specific area.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:174px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiGarbageDump.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/1/10/DFwikiGarbageDump.png" decoding="async" width="172" height="44" class="thumbimage" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiGarbageDump.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The garbage dump icon in-game.</div></div></div>
<p>Press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span>, click on "Garbage Dump", and create a 1×1 activity zone somewhere near your stoneworker's and mechanic's workshops. Unlike stockpile areas where you are limited to storing one object per tile, any number of items may be piled in a garbage area. That means you will only need one tile to hold as much "garbage" as you like.  Although many of the room sizes in this guide are suggestions, think of the 1×1 garbage dump size as mandatory.  At some point you will probably want to retrieve an important item from your garbage dump, and the more tiles your dump contains, the harder it will be to find anything in it. Press <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">i</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span> to select the mass dump/forbid tool. Select a rectangle over the loose stones cluttering up your living area (if there are any – this often isn't a problem yet if you've built your fort in a soil layer). This will designate this stone to be transported to a garbage dump zone. Be sure not to designate the stone in your stockpiles by mistake, since that will only cause your dwarves to perform unnecessary hauling. Once the stone from your living area has been moved there, it will be set as <a href="/index.php/Forbid" title="Forbid">forbidden</a>. Before it can be used you will need to unforbid it using <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">i</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-f">F</span></span> (or just <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">i</span></span>). Note that dwarves hauling stone (or any large, heavy objects) move slowly, and can take a lot of time to reach their destination. This can be a major waste of time if you designate 50 boulders to be dumped at once. Unless the stone is in the way of something, you don't <i>need</i> to dump it every time you dig out a new area. Stones lying on the ground don't slow dwarves down at all. If there is a particular dwarf you don't want hauling "garbage", use the labor menu (<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">y</span></span>) and select the "Haulers" work detail. From there you can select certain dwarves that you want to haul items. By default, Haulers is set to "Everybody does this". You might want to exclude Miners from hauling, since they are far more useful when digging than when moving the stone they just dug out.
</p><p>Congratulations! Knowing how to use garbage dump zones puts you head and shoulders above many new players - it takes some people weeks to figure this out.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trading">Trading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Trading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Not all embark sites have all the resources you need for a successful fortress, but every site has <i>something</i> you can sell. A talented dwarf can process any useless resource into something valuable, and <a href="/index.php/Trading" title="Trading">trading</a> is a good way to sell those goods.
</p><p><i>Note that producing goods creates <a href="/index.php/Wealth" title="Wealth">wealth</a> and getting too much wealth too fast can have <a href="/index.php/Immigration#Migrant_wave_sizes" title="Immigration">unwanted</a> <a href="/index.php/Siege" title="Siege">consequences</a>.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trade_Depot">Trade Depot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Trade Depot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3><p>
Build a <a href="/index.php/Trade_depot" title="Trade depot">trade depot</a> using <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bT.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bT.png" src="/images/9/92/Ui_bT.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="Shift-t">T</span></span></span></span></span> in the 5×5 room you created near your entrance. This is where <a href="/index.php/Caravan" title="Caravan">caravans</a> will park their stuff and where <a href="/index.php/Trading" title="Trading">trading</a> will take place when one arrives. (as stated earlier, the wagons are 3×3 so the entrance tunnel needs to be at least 3×3 for the wagons to go by). You need at least 3 logs or boulders to build the depot. </p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiTradeDepotExample.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/9/97/DFwikiTradeDepotExample.png/300px-DFwikiTradeDepotExample.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="338" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/9/97/DFwikiTradeDepotExample.png 1.5x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiTradeDepotExample.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An example Trade Depot.</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Producing_for_export">Producing for export</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Producing for export">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>While there are some goods that are more valuable, and some that are less valuable, it's a good idea to simply produce/export what you have too much of and to import what you have too little of. 
Generally though, <a href="/index.php/Gem" title="Gem">Gems</a> and <a href="/index.php/Finished_goods" title="Finished goods">Finished goods</a> are decent exports for a new player.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trading_2">Trading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Trading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Once a caravan has arrived, you can mark the goods you want to sell through the Trade Depot, and your dwarves will begin moving them to the depot. Be careful not to sell wooden items to <a href="/index.php/Elf" title="Elf">Elves</a>; <b>this includes containers:</b> even a wooden bin full of metal crafts will make them upset. The same applies to items made of bone and shell (as those involve animal harm). Also note that the traders will want to make a profit off of you. While they're happy with about 200%, the more profit they make on your site, the more goods they will bring next time, so it can be a good idea to give them even better deals.
</p><p><i>A more detailed overview of the entire process is <a href="/index.php/Trading#Trading_Flowchart" title="Trading">here</a>.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="What_to_buy">What to buy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: What to buy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In your first fortress, your priority should be importing some <a href="/index.php/Food" title="Food">food</a> and <a href="/index.php/Alcohol" title="Alcohol">alcohol</a>. In addition, you might want more <a href="/index.php/Meat_industry" title="Meat industry">livestock</a>, <a href="/index.php/Seed" title="Seed">seeds</a> (comes with a free bag), and - depending on what resources you are missing - additional <a href="/index.php/Pick" title="Pick">picks</a>, <a href="/index.php/Barrel" title="Barrel">barrels</a>, <a href="/index.php/Wood" title="Wood">wood</a>, <a href="/index.php/Bag" title="Bag">bags</a>, as well as <a href="/index.php/Rope" class="mw-redirect" title="Rope">rope</a> and a <a href="/index.php/Bucket" title="Bucket">bucket</a> (for a well). While you're at it, check if you need an <a href="/index.php/Anvil" title="Anvil">anvil</a>. Maybe you forgot to bring one, or a <a href="/index.php/Kea" title="Kea">kea</a> stole it. Always having a small supply of <i>all 3 kinds</i> of <a href="/index.php/Cloth" title="Cloth">cloth</a>, some <a href="/index.php/Gem" title="Gem">gems</a>, <a href="/index.php/Leather" title="Leather">leather</a>, a bit of <a href="/index.php/Sand" title="Sand">sand</a> (free bag!) are handy to have, as those are hard to come by on short notice.
If you're short on weapons-grade <a href="/index.php/Metal" title="Metal">metal</a> for your military, import not only actual metal <a href="/index.php/Bar" title="Bar">bars</a> and <a href="/index.php/Ore" title="Ore">ores</a>, buy <i>all</i> metal goods you can afford and <a href="/index.php/Melt_item" title="Melt item">melt</a> them down in a <a href="/index.php/Smelter" title="Smelter">smelter</a> to increase your yield.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Troubleshooting">Troubleshooting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Troubleshooting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Once the depot is built, make sure your depot is accessible. There needs to be a 3-wide passage from the depot to the edge of the map.
</p><p>If you see the message <a href="/index.php/Their_wagons_have_bypassed_your_inaccessible_site" title="Their wagons have bypassed your inaccessible site">Their wagons have bypassed your inaccessible site</a> when the merchants arrive, try these solutions:
</p>
<ul><li>Is the path to the depot (in your fortress) less than 3 tiles wide? If so, expand the entranceway and try again.</li>
<li>Are there <a href="/index.php/Tree" title="Tree">trees</a> blocking a path to the depot outside? Try clearing a path by cutting down a few.</li>
<li>Are there <a href="/index.php/Boulder" title="Boulder">boulders</a> (<span style="color: #C0C0C0; background: #000000; font-size: 135%; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, &#39;Quicktype Mono&#39;, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Lucida Console&#39;, &#39;Lucida Sans Typewriter&#39;, monospace; font-weight:bold; padding: 0; line-height: 1;">∞</span>) blocking the path outside? To remove them easily, you need a <a href="/index.php/Stonecutter" title="Stonecutter">stonecutter</a>. If you selected "play now", you should have one already. Use <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">v</span></span> to smooth stone and designate the boulder(s) for smoothing. They should flash this symbol: <span style="color: #FFFFFF; background: #000000; font-size: 135%; font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;, &#39;Quicktype Mono&#39;, &#39;Bitstream Vera Sans Mono&#39;, &#39;Lucida Console&#39;, &#39;Lucida Sans Typewriter&#39;, monospace; font-weight:bold; padding: 0; line-height: 1;">┼</span></li>
<li>Is the path to the depot only accessible via stairs or did you build traps in the way? Wagons cannot pass traps or stairs, even if they're 3×3 wide.</li>
<li>Building a paved <a href="/index.php/Road" title="Road">road</a> <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bn.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bn.png" src="/images/c/c7/Ui_bn.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">n</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bno.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bno.png" src="/images/e/ef/Ui_bno.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">o</span></span></span></span></span> will stop trees from growing on the wagon path, and can be a good way to ensure that the wagons have an unobstructed path to your depot.</li></ul>
<p>It's possible that there are multiple obstacles blocking the depot, so this can take some troubleshooting.
</p><p><br />
<i>The first few times the traders arrive, they will not bring a wagon anyway. They will only start to bring a wagon once your fortress is a <a href="/index.php/Barony" class="mw-redirect" title="Barony">barony</a>. Without a wagon, they will carry much less goods and you can sell them much less, because their carrying capacity is greatly reduced.</i>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Migrants">Migrants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Migrants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="color: #C0C0C0; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;Terminal&#39;, Consolas, monospace; font-size: 12.5px; background:#000; width: 50em;">Some migrants have arrived.</div>
<p>At some point soon, you'll most likely be getting migrants (if you haven't already). You'll usually get between 5 and 15 migrants in the first 2 waves, which occur sometime during your second and third seasons. See <a href="/index.php/Quickstart_guide/Migrants" title="Quickstart guide/Migrants">this page</a> for advice when you receive migrants.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Bedrooms">Bedrooms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Bedrooms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Up to this point, your dwarves have probably been sleeping on dirt or rock in your fortress. While this is fine for a short time, your dwarves will gradually become less happy if they are forced to sleep without a bed. Under normal circumstances beds can only be made from wood, so be sure to designate some more trees to be cut down if you're short on logs.
</p><p><a href="/index.php/Bedroom_design" title="Bedroom design">Designing living quarters</a> is largely a matter of personal preference and aesthetic sense. While a few useful designs are discussed here, there are many other options. In general, try to keep the bedrooms close to the stairs, and make your access hallways at least two tiles wide to reduce congestion. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Location">Location</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Location">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="metadata plainlinks ambox ambox-content" style="background-color:#fc9;" role="presentation">
<tbody><tr><td class="mbox-empty-cell"></td><td class="mbox-text" style=""><span class="mbox-text-span">This section was migrated from <a href="/index.php/DF2014:Quickstart_guide" title="DF2014:Quickstart guide">DF2014:Quickstart guide</a> and may be inaccurate for the current version of DF (v50.14). See <a href="/index.php/Dwarf_Fortress_Wiki:Version_migration" title="Dwarf Fortress Wiki:Version migration">this page</a> for more information.<span class="hide-when-compact">  </span><span class="hide-when-compact"> </span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Because noise generated from certain jobs (especially mining and woodcutting) can bother sleeping dwarves, doing these jobs within 8 tiles of a sleeping dwarf should be avoided (see <a href="/index.php/Noise" title="Noise">noise</a> for more information). There are two ways of accomplishing this:
</p>
<ul><li>Placing bedrooms at the end of a hallway at least 8 tiles long will avoid most noise (as long as you are careful to avoid noisy jobs directly above or below the bedrooms).</li>
<li>Extending your fortress down several z-levels will also work (9 levels from the surface is a safe choice), although extending a 3×3 staircase takes more work than extending a single hallway.</li></ul>
<p>Both options work equally well, as long as you are careful to avoid disturbing sleeping dwarves. Ultimately it depends on how you want your fortress to look. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Layout">Layout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Layout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Due to the limited resources of a new fortress, setting up a communal sleeping area in a dormitory is often the best short-term solution. However, you can also set up individual bedrooms for dwarves.
</p><p><b>Benefits of individual bedrooms:</b>
</p>
<ul><li>Dwarves are happier with their own bedroom and furniture.</li>
<li>Individual rooms can increase your fort's perceived wealth.</li></ul>
<p><b>Benefits of dormitories:</b>
</p>
<ul><li>Dormitories are easier to set up and expand (only one room is necessary, and each dwarf only requires one bed).</li>
<li>Sleeping dwarves are much less likely to be attacked when other dwarves are around them.</li>
<li>Multiple dwarves can sleep in a dormitory. In contrast, only one dwarf can ever sleep in a bedroom (dwarves cannot sleep in another dwarf's bedroom, even when unoccupied).</li>
<li>Far fewer beds are needed – in a fort of 50 dwarves, for example, around five dwarves will be sleeping at a time (on average). A dormitory, therefore, rarely requires above ten beds, while individual bedrooms would require 50 beds to be built.</li>
<li>Even when all of the beds are occupied, dwarves will still sleep in the general area of the dormitory. This is more convenient than having dwarves sleeping all over your fort.</li></ul>
<p>For now, setting up a dormitory is easiest (although you can change this later, if you feel the need to).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Building">Building</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Building">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Queue up as many beds as you need in a carpenter's workshop (no more than 3 or 4 should be necessary for a dormitory). Build the beds with <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">f</span>-<span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span>. You can check "Keep building after placement" to place multiple beds. (As long as your furniture/general-purpose stockpile isn't full yet, dwarves will store beds in them as they are finished, so there may be a delay before they're available to be built.)
</p><p><b>Setting up a dormitory:</b>
</p>
<ol><li>Dig out an empty room in the location you selected.</li>
<li>Open the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span>one menu and click on "Dormitory". Draw a rectangle over the room you dug out.</li>
<li>Once you have a bed ready, build it anywhere in your dormitory.</li></ol>
<p>You can place multiple beds in the dormitory.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DfwikiIndividualBedroomsQuickstart.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/3/3b/DfwikiIndividualBedroomsQuickstart.png/300px-DfwikiIndividualBedroomsQuickstart.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="300" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/3/3b/DfwikiIndividualBedroomsQuickstart.png 1.5x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DfwikiIndividualBedroomsQuickstart.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>An example of individual bedrooms (with furniture, discussed below)</div></div></div>
<p><b>Setting up individual bedrooms:</b>
</p>
<ol><li>Dig out a small room for each bed (the size and shape are up to you, but 2 to 4 tiles generally works best).</li>
<li>Build each bed <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bf.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bf.png" src="/images/b/b0/Ui_bf.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">f</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bfb.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bfb.png" src="/images/5/5d/Ui_bfb.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span></span> in a room when ready</li>
<li>Make sure each room is enclosed by a door <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bp.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bp.png" src="/images/a/ae/Ui_bp.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">p</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bpr.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bpr.png" src="/images/7/77/Ui_bpr.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">r</span></span></span></span></span>. You can make doors at the carpenter's or stoneworker's workshops.</li>
<li>Open the <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">z</span></span>one menu, and click on "Bedroom".</li>
<li>Click "Multi" (instead of "Paint"), and draw a rectangle containing multiple bedrooms. Each room with a bed, enclosed by a door, will be marked as a bedroom.</li></ol>
<p>You should see <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Current owner: Nobody</span> in the menu. A dwarf will eventually get around to claiming the bedroom – you don't need to assign each dwarf to a specific bedroom.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nobles_and_Administrators">Nobles and Administrators</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Nobles and Administrators">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Hit the <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_n.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui n.png" src="/images/7/7b/Ui_n.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="36" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">n</span></span></span></span></span> key to open up the <a href="/index.php/Noble" title="Noble">nobles and administrators</a> screen.  The most important positions to assign are <b><a href="/index.php/Manager" title="Manager">manager</a></b>, <b><a href="/index.php/Broker" title="Broker">broker</a></b>, and <b><a href="/index.php/Bookkeeper" title="Bookkeeper">bookkeeper</a></b>. 
</p>
<ul><li>A <b>manager</b> will allow you to queue up <a href="/index.php/Work_order" class="mw-redirect" title="Work order">work order</a>, which will greatly simplify managing your production.</li>
<li>A <b>bookkeeper</b> will allow you to maintain inventory counts on the stoc<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">k</span></span>s screen so you'll know what you do and don't have.</li>
<li>A <b>broker</b> is necessary to trade with a caravan once one has arrived at your <a href="/index.php/Trade_depot" title="Trade depot">trade depot</a>.</li></ul>
<h3><span id="Manager_&amp;_Broker"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Manager_.26_Broker">Manager &amp; Broker</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Manager &amp; Broker">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the default <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Play Now!</span> party, your <a href="/index.php/Expedition_leader" title="Expedition leader">expedition leader</a> is a good choice for manager and broker when starting out. Don't worry that it's just one dwarf doing all this; the manager job doesn't take very long, and this dwarf will be available to talk to the traders when a trade delegation arrives.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bookkeeper">Bookkeeper</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Bookkeeper">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the default <span style="color: #C0C0C0; font-size: 12.5px; font-family: &#39;fixedsys&#39;, &#39;IBM Plex Mono Medium&#39;, &#39;Consolas&#39;, monospace; background: #000000">Play Now!</span> party, your planter is a good choice for bookkeeper when starting out.
</p>
<dl><dd><i>See <a href="/index.php/Stocks" title="Stocks">Stocks</a> for a detailed explanation of the stoc<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; -o-border-radius: 0.2em; -ms-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; -webkit-box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; box-shadow: 0.1em 0.2em 0.2em #ddd; background-color: #f9f9f9; background-image: -moz-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -o-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: -webkit-linear-gradient(top, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); background-image: linear-gradient(to bottom, #eee, #f9f9f9, #eee); padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">k</span></span>s screen.</i></dd></dl>
<p>Don't worry about the <a href="/index.php/Chief_medical_dwarf" title="Chief medical dwarf">chief medical dwarf</a> yet. They will be needed when you set up your <a href="/index.php/Healthcare" class="mw-redirect" title="Healthcare">hospital</a> which won't be covered in this guide. Feel free to go check out the <a href="/index.php/Healthcare" class="mw-redirect" title="Healthcare">Healthcare</a> guide once you're done.
</p>
<h3><span id="Offices_(Studies)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Offices_.28Studies.29">Offices (Studies)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=Quickstart_guide&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Offices (Studies)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Some of your administrative positions (manager and bookkeeper) require an <a href="/index.php/Office" title="Office">office</a> in order to function. If your manager, for example, doesn't have an office, you will not be able to do any of the things that require a manager even though you have one assigned. 
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiNoblesScreen.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="/images/thumb/a/a0/DFwikiNoblesScreen.png/400px-DFwikiNoblesScreen.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="169" class="thumbimage" srcset="/images/thumb/a/a0/DFwikiNoblesScreen.png/600px-DFwikiNoblesScreen.png 1.5x, /images/thumb/a/a0/DFwikiNoblesScreen.png/800px-DFwikiNoblesScreen.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/index.php/File:DFwikiNoblesScreen.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Nobles screen. The red stuff turns green once an office is assigned.</div></div></div>
<p>Earlier you should have queued up a table and throne in your stoneworker's shop, and they should be done by now. 
</p>
<ol><li>Dig out a room near your sleeping quarters or stockpiles (at least 1×3, no more than 5×5).</li>
<li>Place the furniture in it with <span><span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_b.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui b.png" src="/images/b/b1/Ui_b.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">b</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bf.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bf.png" src="/images/b/b0/Ui_bf.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em; padding: 0.1em 0.3em; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.9em;" title="">f</span></span></span></span>-<span style="display: inline-flex;"><a href="/index.php/File:Ui_bft.png" class="image"><img alt="Ui bft.png" src="/images/8/8a/Ui_bft.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="32" /></a><span style="align-self: flex-end; margin-left: -3px; margin-bottom: 0px;"><span style="white-space: nowrap;"><span class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; border-radius: 0.2em; -webkit-border-radius: 0.2em; -moz-border-radius: 0.2em;
